### IsSupportedFixedPointType()

Verifies if the input/output/parameter is a supported fixed point type. For now all fixed point types for which the corresponding C api type is a base type are supported.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI.ModelSupport](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-modelsupport.html)

public bool IsSupportedFixedPointType()

#### Returns

True if it is a supported fixed point type, false otherwise.

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| IsSupportedFixedPointType() | Verifies if the input/output/parameter is a supported fixed point type. For now all fixed point types for which the corresponding C api type is a base type are supported. |
| IsValid() | Verifies if the input/output/parameter is valid based on VeriStand's current support. |

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns int dimensions for the current item. Scalar and multidimensional array have dimensions contained into an array, but the unidimensional array only has a scalar value (length of the array). We consider unidimensional array to have dimensions: [N, 1]. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriSt

### GetDimensions(object)

Returns int dimensions for the current item. Scalar and multidimensional array have dimensions contained into an array, but the unidimensional array only has a scalar value (length of the array). We consider unidimensional array to have dimensions: [N, 1].

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI.ModelSupport](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-modelsupport.html)

public static int[] GetDimensions(object dimensions)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| dimensions | object | dimensions data read from JSON |

#### Returns

array of dimensions

### ModeTimeDifference Class

## TOPIC 03324: NodeIDUtil Class

- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-nodeidutil.html`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Provides methods for converting node IDs, or pointers, to nodes in a system definition file into item references to the same node. Derives fromNoneSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class NodeIDUtilRemarksUse the members of this class to access node-specific cla

### NodeIDUtil Class

Provides methods for converting node IDs, or pointers, to nodes in a system definition file into item references to the same node.

#### Derives from

None

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class NodeIDUtil

#### Remarks

CustomDevice

CustomDeviceChannel

Note

If you are programming in LabVIEW, you can use the members of this class to switch between the .NET API and the NI VeriStand VIs available in LabVIEW. The .NET API often uses node IDs where the LabVIEW VIs use node references.

**Accessing this Class**

- NodeIDUtil Constructor

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| IDToBaseNode(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a BaseNode object. This method attempts to type cast based on the GUID of the node. |
| IDToCustomDevice(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a CustomDevice object. |
| IDToCustomDeviceBase(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a CustomDeviceBase object. |
| IDToCustomDeviceChannel(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a CustomDeviceChannel object. |
| IDToCustomDeviceSection(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a CustomDeviceSection object. |
| IDToCustomDeviceWaveform(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a CustomDeviceWaveform object. |
| IDToTimingSyncDevice(ulong) | Converts the specified nodeID to a TimingAndSyncDevice object. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

### GetUnconditional()

Accesses the [Unconditional](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-unconditional.html) class, which you can use to add outgoing unconditional frames under an NI-XNET LIN port. Unconditional frames are the most common type of outgoing LIN frame and carry signals, or data.

## TOPIC 03331: Outgoing Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-outgoing.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-outgoing.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents the Outgoing section under an NI-XNET CAN, LIN, or FlexRay port, which contains any outgoing frames and data replay files. Derives fromSectionSectionSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class Outgoing : Section, SectionRemarksUse the members of this cla

### Outgoing Class

Represents the **Outgoing** section under an NI-XNET CAN, LIN, or FlexRay port, which contains any outgoing frames and data replay files.

#### Derives from

- Section
- Section

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class Outgoing : Section, Section

#### Remarks

Use the members of this class to access various types of outgoing frames, such as cyclic, event triggered, sporadic, and unconditional. You also can access data replay files, which are log files that replay onto a CAN bus.

**Accessing this Class**

- [GetOutgoing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-canport-getoutgoing.html)
- [GetOutgoing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-linport-getoutgoing.html)
- [GetOutgoing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-flexrayport-getoutgoing.html)

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GetCyclic() | Accesses the Cyclic class, which you can use to add outgoing cyclic frames under an NI-XNET CAN or FlexRay port. |
| GetCyclicEvent() | Accesses the CyclicEvent class, which you can use to add outgoing cyclic/event frames under an NI-XNET CAN port. |
| GetDataReplay() | Accesses the DataReplay class, which you can use to add TDMS (.tdms) or NI-XNET data log (.ncl) files for replay onto a CAN bus. |
| GetEventTriggered() | Accesses the EventTriggered class, which you can use to add outgoing event triggered frames under an NI-XNET CAN or FlexRay port. |
| GetSporadic() | Accesses the Sporadic class, which you can use to add outgoing sporadic frames under an NI-XNET LIN port. Sporadic frames attempt to provide dynamic behavior to LIN. |
| GetUnconditional() | Accesses the Unconditional class, which you can use to add outgoing unconditional frames under an NI-XNET LIN port. Unconditional frames are the most common type of outgoing LIN frame and carry signals, or data. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

### OutputUnderflowChannel Class

Represents an output underflow count channel, which tracks the number of times the system fails to read data from an asynchronous custom device because there is no data to read. A single custom device can have only one output underflow count channel.

- CustomDeviceChannel

### ParameterAccess Enumeration

Defines the parameter access mode on the engine. The user can select to access only the imported parameters or all the parameters from the models.

#### Syntax

public enum ParameterAccess

#### Members

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| OnlyImportedParameters | 0 | Only allow reading and writing imported parameters. |
| AnyParameter | 1 | Allow reading and writing any parameter. |

## TOPIC 03352: PeakAndValley Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-peakandvalley.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-peakandvalley.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a calculated channel with the Peak & Valley function. This function calculates the peak, valley, and offset of a cyclical waveform on the channel you specify. The calculated channel stores the peak value, and the channels you specify when you configure the calculated channel store the val

### PeakAndValley Class

Represents a calculated channel with the **Peak & Valley** function. This function calculates the peak, valley, and offset of a cyclical waveform on the channel you specify. The calculated channel stores the peak value, and the channels you specify when you configure the calculated channel store the valley and offset values.

#### Derives from

- CalculatedChannel

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class PeakAndValley : CalculatedChannel

#### Remarks

Use the members of this class to get and set the channel to analyze, the channels that store the valley and offset values, and the hysteresis value.

**Accessing this Class**

- PeakAndValley Constructor

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PeakAndValley(string, string, BaseNode, BaseNode, BaseNode, uint, double) | Initializes a new instance of PeakAndValley with the specified name, description, and configuration. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ChannelForOffset | Gets or sets the channel on which to store the offset value. |
| ChannelForValley | Gets or sets the channel on which to store the valley value. |
| ChannelToAnalyze | Gets or sets the channel for which to calculate the peak, valley, and offset. |
| Hysteresis | Gets or sets the amount by which the value of ChannelToAnalyze must exceed the Reset value for the calculation to reset. |
| Reset | Gets or sets the value at which to reset the calculation. If the ChannelToAnalyze surpasses this value by more than the specified Hysteresis, the calculation resets. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=veristand-net-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-pendingframes.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 03353: PendingFrames Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-pendingframes.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-pendingframes.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a Pending Frames channel associate with an NI-XNET DataFileReplay file. This channel stores the number of frames in the outgoing transmission queue of the current NI-XNET streaming session. You can use this channel to determine whether data is replaying as expected. Derives fromChannelSyn

### PendingFrames Class

Represents a **Pending Frames** channel associate with an NI-XNET [DataFileReplay](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafilereplay.html) file. This channel stores the number of frames in the outgoing transmission queue of the current NI-XNET streaming session. You can use this channel to determine whether data is replaying as expected.

#### Derives from

- Channel

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class PendingFrames : Channel

#### Remarks

**Data is Replaying Correctly**

- If the value of Pending Frames is changing, the value of [DataFileStatus](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafilestatus.html) is true, and the value of [DataFileError](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafileerror.html) is 0 (no error), data is replaying correctly.
- If the value of Pending Frames is a non-zero number that is not changing, the value of [DataFileStatus](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafilestatus.html) is true, and the value of [DataFileError](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafileerror.html) is 0 (no error), data is replaying, but you might need to reduce the number of frames you are adding for replay or the rate at which you are adding them. The output queue for streaming has a limited size, and you might be attempting to stream too much data too quickly.
- If the value of Pending Frames is 0, the value of [DataFileStatus](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafilestatus.html) was true but changes to false, and the value of [DataFileError](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafileerror.html) is 0 (no error), data replay has completed.

**Data is Not Replaying Correctly**

- If the value of Pending Frames is 0, the value of [DataFileStatus](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafilestatus.html) is true, and the value of [DataFileError](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafileerror.html) is 0 (no error), you have exceeded the size of the outgoing buffer. Data is not replaying correctly. Reduce the number of frames you are attempting to write to the output stream in a single chunk.
- If the value of [DataFileError](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datafileerror.html) is anything other than 0, data is not replaying correctly, regardless of the Pending Frames value.

Note

The replay process creates this channel. You cannot directly call this class.

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

An array of the forward coefficients in the form of a0, a1, a2,...a*n* for the polynomial scale *y* = a0 + a1*x* + a2*x*<sup>2</sup> + … + a*nx<sup>n</sup>*, where *y* is the scaled data and *x* is the raw data.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=veristand-net-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-polynomialscale.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 03358: PolynomialScale Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-polynomialscale.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-polynomialscale.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a polynomial Scale, which converts values using a polynomial equation with up to ten coefficients. Derives fromScaleSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class PolynomialScale : ScaleRemarksNI VeriStand requires both a polynomial to convert pre-scaled va

### PolynomialScale Class

Represents a polynomial [Scale](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-scale.html), which converts values using a polynomial equation with up to ten coefficients.

#### Derives from

- Scale

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class PolynomialScale : Scale

#### Remarks

NI VeriStand requires both a polynomial to convert pre-scaled values to scaled values (forward) and a polynomial to convert scaled values to pre-scaled values (reverse). For example, suppose you want to relate pre-scaled values to scaled values according to the following polynomial scale:

*y* = *x*<sup>2</sup> + *x* + 0

For input operations, if the device acquires a pre-scaled value of 2, the scaled value that is read is 6. For output operations, if you write a scaled value of 6, the device generates a value of 2.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PolynomialScale(string, double[], double[], string) | Initializes a new instance of the PolynomialScale class with the specified name and properties. |
| PolynomialScale(string) | Initializes a new instance of the PolynomialScale class with the specified name. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PolynomialCoeff | Gets or sets the forward coefficients of the PolynomialScale. |
| ReversePolynomialCoeff | Gets or sets the reverse coefficients of the PolynomialScale. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

## TOPIC 03361: AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmingStepFunction, BaseNode, out Error)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure-addnewalarming__string-string-alarmingstepfunction-basenode-out.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure-addnewalarming__string-string-alarmingstepfunction-basenode-out.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adds a new Alarming step to a procedure. This step performs the specified Function on the specified Alarm when the step executes. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic bool AddNewAlarming(string Name, string Description, AlarmingStepFunction Function, BaseNode Alar

### AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmingStepFunction, BaseNode, out Error)

Adds a new [Alarming](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-alarming.html) step to a procedure. This step performs the specified *Function*  on the specified *Alarm*  when the step executes.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public bool AddNewAlarming(string Name, string Description, AlarmingStepFunction Function, BaseNode Alarm, out Error error)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | string | The name of the step. |
| Description | string | The description of the step. |
| Function | AlarmingStepFunction | The action that the step performs on the Alarm . |
| Alarm | BaseNode | The alarm on which to apply the Function . |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

#### Returns

true if the [Alarming](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-alarming.html) step was added successfully.

Parent topic:

Procedure Class

## TOPIC 03363: AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmPriority, AlarmState, BaseNode, double, BaseNode, BaseNode, BaseNode, BaseNode, out Error)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure-addnewalarming__string-string-alarmpriority-alarmstate-basenode-double-basenode-basenode-basenode-basenode-out.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure-addnewalarming__string-string-alarmpriority-alarmstate-basenode-double-basenode-basenode-basenode-basenode-out.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adds a new Alarming step and applies the specified settings to the Alarm . This method uses channel values to specify the upper and lower limits of the alarm. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic bool AddNewAlarming(string Name, string Description, AlarmPriority P

### AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmPriority, AlarmState, BaseNode, double, BaseNode, BaseNode, BaseNode, BaseNode, out Error)

Adds a new [Alarming](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-alarming.html) step and applies the specified settings to the *Alarm* . This method uses channel values to specify the upper and lower limits of the alarm.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public bool AddNewAlarming(string Name, string Description, AlarmPriority Priority, AlarmState DefaultState, BaseNode Alarm, double Delay, BaseNode Procedure, BaseNode AlarmChannel, BaseNode UpperLimit, BaseNode LowerLimit, out Error error)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | string | The name of the step. |
| Description | string | The description of the step. |
| Priority | AlarmPriority | The priority level of the alarm. |
| DefaultState | AlarmState | The default state of the alarm. |
| Alarm | BaseNode | The alarm to apply settings to. |
| Delay | double | The amount of time to wait before triggering the alarm. |
| Procedure | BaseNode | The procedure to initiate when the alarm occurs. |
| AlarmChannel | BaseNode | The channel to monitor for alarm conditions. |
| UpperLimit | BaseNode | The channel that determines the high limit value of the alarm. If the value of AlarmSource exceeds this limit, the alarm is triggered. |
| LowerLimit | BaseNode | The channel that determines the low limit value of the alarm. If the value of AlarmSource falls below this limit, the alarm is triggered. |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

#### Returns

true if the [Alarming](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-alarming.html) step was added successfully.

Parent topic:

Procedure Class

- source_description: Adds a new Alarming step and applies the specified settings to the Alarm . This method uses constant values to specify the upper and lower limits of the alarm. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic bool AddNewAlarming(string Name, string Description, AlarmPriority

### AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmPriority, AlarmState, BaseNode, double, BaseNode, BaseNode, double, double)

Adds a new [Alarming](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-alarming.html) step and applies the specified settings to the *Alarm* . This method uses constant values to specify the upper and lower limits of the alarm.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public bool AddNewAlarming(string Name, string Description, AlarmPriority Priority, AlarmState DefaultState, BaseNode Alarm, double Delay, BaseNode Procedure, BaseNode AlarmChannel, double UpperLimit, double LowerLimit)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | string | The name of the step. |
| Description | string | The description of the step. |
| Priority | AlarmPriority | The priority level of the alarm. |
| DefaultState | AlarmState | The default state of the alarm. |
| Alarm | BaseNode | The alarm to apply settings to. |
| Delay | double | The amount of time to wait before triggering the alarm. |
| Procedure | BaseNode | The procedure to initiate when the alarm occurs. |
| AlarmChannel | BaseNode | The channel to monitor for alarm conditions. |
| UpperLimit | double | The constant that determines the high limit value of the alarm. If the value of AlarmSource exceeds this limit, the alarm is triggered. |
| LowerLimit | double | The constant that determines the low limit value of the alarm. If the value of AlarmSource falls below this limit, the alarm is triggered. |

#### Returns

true if the [Alarming](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-alarming.html) step was added successfully.

Parent topic:

Procedure Class

- source_description: Adds a new Condition step. This step compares Variable to Value and, if the Comparison condition is met, jumps to the procedure step specified by GotoLabel . This method uses a channel to specify the Value parameter. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic bool AddNe

### AddNewCondition(string, string, BaseNode, ConditionStepComparison, BaseNode, Command, out Error)

Adds a new [Condition](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-condition.html) step. This step compares *Variable*  to *Value*  and, if the *Comparison*  condition is met, jumps to the procedure step specified by *GotoLabel* . This method uses a channel to specify the *Value*  parameter.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public bool AddNewCondition(string Name, string Description, BaseNode Variable, ConditionStepComparison Comparison, BaseNode Value, Command GotoLabel, out Error error)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | string | The name of the step. |
| Description | string | The description of the step. |
| Variable | BaseNode | The channel in the system to use to compare with Value. |
| Comparison | ConditionStepComparison | The condition to use when comparing Variable and Value. |
| Value | BaseNode | The channel value to compare with Variable. |
| GotoLabel | Command | The procedure step to jump to when the Comparison condition is met. |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

#### Returns

true if the [Condition](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-condition.html) step was added successfully.

Parent topic:

Procedure Class

### AddNewExitSubroutine(string, string, out Error)

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public bool AddNewExitSubroutine(string Name, string Description, out Error error)

#### Remarks

Adds a new [ExitSubroutine](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-exitsubroutine.html) step. This step exits a procedure that you call from another procedure using a [CallProcedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-callprocedure.html) step and returns to the calling procedure.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | string | The name of the step. |
| Description | string | The description of the step. |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

#### Returns

true if the [ExitSubroutine](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-exitsubroutine.html) step was added successfully.

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic RealTimeSequenceCommand AddNewRealTimeSequenceCommand(string name, string description, GlobalSequ

### AddNewRealTimeSequenceCommand(string, string, GlobalSequenceCommand, bool, double, bool, int, out Error)

Adds a new [RealTimeSequenceCommand](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-realtimesequencecommand.html) step that performs the *sequenceCommand*  command you specify on all running real-time sequences.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public [RealTimeSequenceCommand](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-realtimesequencecommand.html) AddNewRealTimeSequenceCommand(string name, string description, GlobalSequenceCommand sequenceCommand, bool waitForSequencesToComplete, double waitTimeout, bool abortSequencesOnTimeout, int groupNumber, out Error error)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | string | The name of the step. |
| description | string | The description of the step. |
| sequenceCommand | GlobalSequenceCommand | Specifies the sequence command to apply to all running sequences. |
| waitForSequencesToComplete | bool | Specifies whether to wait for all active sequences to complete execution. |
| waitTimeout | double | Specifies the maximum amount of time in seconds to wait for all active sequences to complete execution. |
| abortSequencesOnTimeout | bool | Specifies whether to abort all active sequences if the sequence command times out waiting for them to complete. |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |
| groupNumber | int | Specifies the group number of the sequence to stop. |

#### Returns

Returns the newly created [RealTimeSequenceCommand](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-realtimesequencecommand.html) step.

Parent topic:

Procedure Class

## TOPIC 03395: AddNewSetVariable(string, string, BaseNode, SetVariableStepFunction, BaseNode, BaseNode, out Error)

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure-addnewsetvariable__string-string-basenode-setvariablestepfunction-basenode-basenode-out.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure-addnewsetvariable__string-string-basenode-setvariablestepfunction-basenode-basenode-out.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adds a new SetVariable step that performs the Function you specify on Value1 and Value2 and sets the value of the Variable channel to the result. This method uses channels for the values of Value1 and Value2 . SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic bool AddNewSetVar

### AddNewSetVariable(string, string, BaseNode, SetVariableStepFunction, BaseNode, BaseNode, out Error)

Adds a new [SetVariable](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-setvariable.html) step that performs the *Function*  you specify on *Value1*  and *Value2*  and sets the value of the *Variable*  channel to the result. This method uses channels for the values of *Value1*  and *Value2* .

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public bool AddNewSetVariable(string Name, string Description, BaseNode Variable, SetVariableStepFunction Function, BaseNode Value1, BaseNode Value2, out Error error)

#### Remarks

Note

*Value1*  is always the first term in the *Function*  operation.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Name | string | The name of the step. |
| Description | string | The description of the step. |
| Variable | BaseNode | The channel in the system whose value you want to set. |
| Function | SetVariableStepFunction | The function to apply to Value1 and Value2 . |
| Value1 | BaseNode | The channel that specifies the value of Value1 . |
| Value2 | BaseNode | The channel that specifies the value of Value2 . |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic Command[] GetCommandList()RemarksModifications you make to the co

### GetCommandList()

Gets an array that contains the [Command](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-command.html) elements from the current [Procedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html). This method gets all the steps, or commands, currently configured for the procedure.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public [Command](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-command.html)[] GetCommandList()

#### Remarks

Note

Modifications you make to the contents of this list apply to the system definition. However, modifications you make to the array container, such as by calling Array.SetValue() or Array.Clear(), have no effect on the system definition.

#### Returns

An array that contains the [Command](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-command.html) elements from the current [Procedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html).

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 03407: Procedure Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a procedure, which determines a set of actions that the VeriStand Engine executes. You can configure procedures to run in response to an alarm, when called from another procedure, or on startup. Derives fromSectionSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic cl

### Procedure Class

Represents a procedure, which determines a set of actions that the VeriStand Engine executes. You can configure procedures to run in response to an alarm, when called from another procedure, or on startup.

#### Derives from

- Section

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class Procedure : Section

#### Remarks

Use the members of this class to add steps, or commands, to a procedure, or to get a list of existing commands.

**Accessing this Class**

- M:NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI.Procedures.GetProceduresList

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Procedure(string, string) | Initializes a new instance of Procedure with the specified name and description. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AddCommand(Command, out Error) | Adds the specified Command, or step, to the Procedure. |
| AddCommand(Command) | Adds the specified Command, or step, to the Procedure. |
| AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmPriority, AlarmState, BaseNode, double, BaseNode, BaseNode, double, BaseNode, out Error) | Adds a new Alarming step and applies the specified settings to the Alarm . This method uses a constant value to specify the upper limit of the alarm and a channel value to specify the lower limit. |
| AddNewAlarming(string, string, AlarmPriority, AlarmState, BaseNode, double, BaseNode, BaseNode, BaseNode, double) | Adds a new Alarming step and applies the specified settings to the Alarm . This method uses a channel value to specify the upper limit of the alarm and a constant value to specify the lower limit. |

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Gets an array that contains the Procedure elements from the Procedures section. This method gets the individual procedures in the system definition. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic Procedure[] GetProceduresList()RemarksModifications you make to the contents o

### GetProceduresList()

Gets an array that contains the [Procedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html) elements from the [Procedures](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedures.html) section. This method gets the individual procedures in the system definition.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public [Procedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html)[] GetProceduresList()

#### Remarks

Note

Modifications you make to the contents of this list apply to the system definition. However, modifications you make to the array container, such as by calling Array.SetValue() or Array.Clear(), have no effect on the system definition.

#### Returns

An array that contains the [Procedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html) elements from the [Procedures](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedures.html) section.

Parent topic:

Procedures Class

Derives fromSectionSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class Procedures : SectionRemarksUse the members of this class to add a procedure, get a list of procedur

### Procedures Class

Represents the **Procedures** section of a [Target](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-target.html), which contains all the [Procedure](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-procedure.html) objects you configure.

#### Derives from

- Section

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class Procedures : Section

#### Remarks

Use the members of this class to add a procedure, get a list of procedures, or reorder the execution of a list of procedures.

**Accessing this Class**

- M:NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI.Target.GetProcedures

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| StartupProcedure | Gets or sets a value indicating the procedure that runs on startup. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AddProcedure(Procedure) | Adds the specified procedure to the Procedures section. |
| AddProcedure(Procedure, out Error) | Adds the specified procedure to the Procedures section. |
| GetProceduresList() | Gets an array that contains the Procedure elements from the Procedures section. This method gets the individual procedures in the system definition. |
| ReorderProcedureList(Procedure[]) | Reorders the execution of the procedures in the system. |
| ReorderProcedureList(Procedure[], out Error) | Reorders the execution of the procedures in the system. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

- source_description: Represents a raw data format channel under an NI-XNET RawDataBasedFrame. Derives fromChannelSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class RawDataBasedChannel : ChannelRemarksUse the members of this class to configure settings for a raw data channel, including its def

### RawDataBasedChannel Class

Represents a raw data format channel under an NI-XNET [RawDataBasedFrame](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-rawdatabasedframe.html).

#### Derives from

- Channel

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class RawDataBasedChannel : Channel

#### Remarks

Use the members of this class to configure settings for a raw data channel, including its default value, start bit, and total number of bits.

**Accessing this Class**

- [CreateRawDataBasedChannel(uint, uint, out Error)](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-rawdatabasedframe-createrawdatabasedchannel__uint-uint-out.1.html)
- [GetRawDataBasedChannelList](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-rawdatabasedframe-getrawdatabasedchannellist.html)

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DefaultValue | Gets or sets the default value of the channel. |
| Enable64Bit | Gets or sets whether U64 bitfield representation is enabled for the frame. |
| NumberOfBits | Gets or sets the number of bits the signal uses in the frame payload. |
| StartBit | Gets or sets the start bit, or the least significant signal bit position in the frame payload. This value determines the signal starting point in the frame. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Creates an AutomaticFrameProcessing section under the frame, which contains sections to add a cyclic redundancy check (CRC) and counter. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic AutomaticFrameProcessing CreateAutomaticFrameProcessing(out Error error)RemarksThis method

### CreateAutomaticFrameProcessing(out Error)

Creates an [AutomaticFrameProcessing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-automaticframeprocessing.html) section under the frame, which contains sections to add a cyclic redundancy check (CRC) and counter.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public [AutomaticFrameProcessing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-automaticframeprocessing.html) CreateAutomaticFrameProcessing(out Error error)

#### Remarks

This method is only valid for outgoing CAN/LIN frames. This method does not create a section if the frame is not an outgoing frame of a CAN/LIN port, or if an [AutomaticFrameProcessing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-automaticframeprocessing.html) section already exists under the frame.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

#### Returns

Upon return, contains a reference to the [AutomaticFrameProcessing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-automaticframeprocessing.html) section.

Parent topic:

RawDataBasedFrame Class

### CreateFrameFaulting(bool, bool, out Error)

Creates a [FrameFaulting](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-framefaulting.html) section under the frame, which contains channels you can use to control the transmission of outgoing cyclic frames.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public [FrameFaulting](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-framefaulting.html) CreateFrameFaulting(bool CreateSkipCyclicFrames, bool CreateTransmitTime, out Error error)

#### Remarks

This method is only valid for outgoing cyclic frames under CAN ports. This method does not create a section if the frame is not an outgoing cyclic frame of a CAN port, or if a [FrameFaulting](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-framefaulting.html) section already exists under the frame.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| CreateSkipCyclicFrames | bool | If true, creates a SkipCyclicFrames channel under the section. |
| CreateTransmitTime | bool | If true, creates a TransmitTime channel under the section. |
| error | out Error | Returns an NationalInstruments.VeriStand.Error object. If no error occurs, the Code property of the Error object is 0. |

#### Returns

Upon return, contains a reference to the [FrameFaulting](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-framefaulting.html) section.

## TOPIC 03450: StartTimeOffset

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-rawdatabasedframe-starttimeoffset.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-rawdatabasedframe-starttimeoffset.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Gets or sets the amount of time that elapses between the session start and the transmission of the first frame. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic double StartTimeOffset { get; set; }RemarksThis property is only valid for outgoing cyclic CAN frames. Use this pro

### StartTimeOffset

Gets or sets the amount of time that elapses between the session start and the transmission of the first frame.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public double StartTimeOffset { get; set; }

#### Remarks

This property is only valid for outgoing cyclic CAN frames. Use this property to have more control over the schedule of frames on the bus, and to offer more determinism by configuring cyclic frames to be spaced evenly. If this field contains a negative number, NI-XNET chooses the start time offset based on the arbitration identifier and periodic transmit time.

#### Returns

The start time offset, in seconds.

Parent topic:

RawDataBasedFrame Class

## TOPIC 03454: RawDataBasedFrame Class

- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a raw data format frame of an NI-XNET CAN, LIN, or FlexRay device. Derives fromSectionSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class RawDataBasedFrame : SectionRemarksUse the members of this class get or set information about the frame, such as the XNET dat

### RawDataBasedFrame Class

Represents a raw data format frame of an NI-XNET CAN, LIN, or FlexRay device.

#### Derives from

- Section

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class RawDataBasedFrame : Section

#### Remarks

Use the members of this class get or set information about the frame, such as the XNET database and cluster that contain it, its frame ID number, and any transmission triggers (outgoing frames only).

**Accessing this Class**

- [GetRawDataBasedFrameList](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-cyclic-getrawdatabasedframelist.html)
- [GetRawDataBasedFrameList](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-eventtriggered-getrawdatabasedframelist.html)
- [GetRawDataBasedFrameList](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-singlepoint-getrawdatabasedframelist.html)
- [GetRawDataBasedFrameList](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-sporadic-getrawdatabasedframelist.html)
- [GetRawDataBasedFrameList](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-unconditional-getrawdatabasedframelist.html)
- RawDataBasedFrame Constructor

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| RawDataBasedFrame(string, uint, Database, string, uint, double, bool, string[]) | Initializes a new instance of the RawDataBasedFrame class. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ClusterName | Gets or sets the name of the cluster in the XNET database that contains the frame. |
| DatabaseAlias | Gets or sets the alias for the XNET database that contains the frame. |
| DisableChannel | Gets a reference to the disable channel for the frame. A disable channel disables transmission of an outgoing frame when the value of the disable channel is non-zero. |
| Disabled | Gets whether transmission of the outgoing frame is disabled. |
| Enable64Bit | Gets or sets whether U64 bitfield representation is enabled for the frame. |
| EnableFrameCyclicTrigger | Gets or sets whether a frame cyclic trigger, which transmits outgoing frames when TriggerChannel has a non-zero value, is enabled for the frame. |
| EnableSoftwareCyclicTrigger | Gets or sets whether a software cyclic trigger, which transmits outgoing frames at regular intervals specified by TransmitTime, is enabled for the frame. |
| FrameType | Gets or sets the frame type (CAN data, CAN remote, FlexRay data, or FlexRay null) of a frame under a CAN or FlexRay port. |
| ID | Gets or sets the identifier number for the frame. For LIN frames, this is the frame ID. For CAN frames, this is the Arbitration ID. For FlexRay frames, this is the Slot ID in which the frame is sent. |
| MD5 | Gets the MD5 message digest for the frame. |
| OwningDatabase | Gets or sets a reference to the XNET database that contains the frame. |
| PayloadLength | Gets or sets the number of bytes in the payload of the frame. |
| Phase | Gets or sets whether to reset the timer after the TransmitTime elapses when EnableSoftwareCyclicTrigger is true. |
| StartTimeOffset | Gets or sets the amount of time that elapses between the session start and the transmission of the first frame. |
| TransmitTime | Gets or sets the interval, in seconds, at which a software cyclic trigger transmits outgoing frames when EnableSoftwareCyclicTrigger is true. |
| TransmitTrigger | Gets the trigger type (channel value change, trigger channel not zero, and so on) specified for an event-triggered frame. |
| TriggerChannel | Gets a reference to the channel that is checked for a non-zero value when EnableFrameCyclicTrigger is true. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| CreateAutomaticFrameProcessing(out AutomaticFrameProcessing) | Creates an AutomaticFrameProcessing section under the frame, which contains sections to add a cyclic redundancy check (CRC) and counter. |
| CreateAutomaticFrameProcessing(out Error) | Creates an AutomaticFrameProcessing section under the frame, which contains sections to add a cyclic redundancy check (CRC) and counter. |
| CreateFrameFaulting(bool, bool, out FrameFaulting) | Creates a FrameFaulting section under the frame, which contains channels you can use to control the transmission of outgoing cyclic frames. |
| CreateFrameFaulting(bool, bool, out Error) | Creates a FrameFaulting section under the frame, which contains channels you can use to control the transmission of outgoing cyclic frames. |
| CreateFrameInformation(bool, bool, out FrameInformation) | Creates a FrameInformation section under the frame, which contains channels with timing and ID information for incoming frames. |
| CreateFrameInformation(bool, bool, out Error) | Creates a FrameInformation section under the frame, which contains channels with timing and ID information for incoming frames. |
| CreateRawDataBasedChannel(uint, uint, out RawDataBasedChannel) | Creates a RawDataBasedChannel under the frame. |
| CreateRawDataBasedChannel(uint, uint, out Error) | Creates a RawDataBasedChannel under the frame. |
| DisableTransmissionTrigger() | Disables a transmission trigger previously enabled by EnableTransmissionTrigger. |
| EnableTransmissionTrigger(BaseNode) | Enables checking the value of a DisableChannel to enable or disable transmission of the outgoing frame. |
| GetAutomaticFrameProcessing() | Gets the Automatic Frame Processing section of a frame, which contains the CRC and Counter sections for the frame. |
| GetFrameFaulting() | Gets the Frame Faulting section of the frame, which contains the SkipCyclicFrames and TransmitTime channels for the frame. |
| GetFrameInformation() | Gets the Frame Information section of the frame, which contains the ReceiveTime and TimeDifference channels for the frame. |
| GetRawDataBasedChannelList() | Gets an array that contains the RawDataBasedChannel elements of the current RawDataBasedFrame. This method gets the raw data channels in the frame. |
| SetTransmitTrigger(FrameTriggerType, BaseNode) | Sets event-triggered frame transmission on the frame. |

Parent topic:

| --- | --- |
| RealTimeSequenceCommand() | Initializes a new instance of the RealTimeSequenceCommand class. |
| RealTimeSequenceCommand(string, GlobalSequenceCommand, bool, double, bool, int) | Initializes a new instance of the RealTimeSequenceCommand class with group number. |
| RealTimeSequenceCommand(string, GlobalSequenceCommand, bool, double, bool) | Initializes a new instance of the RealTimeSequenceCommand class. |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AbortSequencesOnTimeout | Gets or sets a value indicating whether to abort all active sequences if the sequence command times out waiting for them to complete. |
| GroupNumber | Gets or sets a value indicating the group number for the sequence to stop. |
| SequenceCommand | Gets or sets a value indicating the global command to apply to all running real-time sequences. |
| WaitForSequencesToComplete | Gets or sets a value indicating whether to wait for all active sequences to complete execution. |
| WaitTimeout | Gets or sets a value indicating the maximum amount of time in seconds to wait for all active sequences to complete execution. |

Parent topic:

### ReceiveTime Class

Represents the **Receive Time** channel for an incoming NI-XNET CAN, LIN, or FlexRay frame. This channel contains the most recent timestamp at which the frame was received.

#### Derives from

- Channel

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class ReceiveTime : Channel

#### Remarks

You can use the members of this class to configure the Receive Time channel and, if you require a dedicated start value, to set the initial receive time.

**Accessing this Class**

- [GetReceiveTime](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-frameinformation-getreceivetime.html)

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| InitialValue | Gets or sets the initial value of the Receive Time channel. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| RemoveNode() | Removes the Receive Time channel from the FrameInformation section, as well as the Time Difference channel, if it exists. |

Parent topic:

This method sends the interrupts to all nodes on the reflective memory network. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic void EnableInterrupt(Refl

### EnableInterrupt(ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType, BaseNode)

Enables interrupts of the *type*  you specify and assigns the interrupt signal the value of the specified *interruptChannel* . This method sends the interrupts to all nodes on the reflective memory network.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public void EnableInterrupt(ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType type, BaseNode interruptChannel)

#### Remarks

All interrupts are sent in packets that contain the node ID of the sender, the node ID of the receiver, the type of the interrupt, and 32 bits of data you define.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| type | ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType | The type of interrupt, such as LinkResetInterrupt or NetworkInitInterrupt, to enable. |
| interruptChannel | BaseNode | The channel to use for the interrupt value. |

Parent topic:

ReflectiveMemory Class

## TOPIC 03487: ReflectiveMemory Class

- bundle_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememory.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/veristand-net-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememory.html
- document_id: `veristand-net-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Represents a reflective memory device under the DataSharing section of the system definition. A reflective memory device is a target on a ReflectiveMemoryNetwork. Derives fromSectionSectionSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPIpublic class ReflectiveMemory : Section, Sect

### ReflectiveMemory Class

Represents a reflective memory device under the [DataSharing](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datasharing.html) section of the system definition. A reflective memory device is a target on a [ReflectiveMemoryNetwork](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememorynetwork.html).

#### Derives from

- Section
- Section

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public class ReflectiveMemory : Section, Section

#### Remarks

NI VeriStand 2010 and later provides native support for GE Fanuc Intelligent Platforms reflective memory boards.

**Accessing this Class**

- [GetReflectiveMemory](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-datasharing-getreflectivememory.html)
- ReflectiveMemory Constructor

#### Thread Safety

Any members of this type are not guaranteed to be thread safe.

#### Constructors

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ReflectiveMemory(string) | Initializes a new instance of the ReflectiveMemory class for the reflective memory device with the specified Name . |

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| GenerateInterrupt | Gets whether interrupts are enabled for the reflective memory device. |
| InterruptAllNodes | Gets whether the device sends interrupt signals to all nodes on the reflective memory network. |
| InterruptChannelData | Gets the channel that provides the data included in the interrupt packet. |
| InterruptConstantData | Gets the constant value that is the data included in the interrupt packet. |
| InterruptDataConstant | Gets whether the data included in the interrupt packet is a constant value. |
| InterruptTargetNode | Gets the decimal ID of the target node to which the reflective memory device sends interrupts. |
| InterruptType | Gets the type of interrupt the reflective memory device generates. |
| VISAResource | Gets or sets the VISA resource name for the device as it appears in Measurement & Automation Explorer (MAX). |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| DisableInterrupt() | Disables the reflective memory device from asserting its interrupt pin. |
| EnableInterrupt(ushort, ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType, BaseNode) | Enables interrupts of the type you specify for the interruptTargetNode you specify, and assigns the interrupt signal the value of the interruptChannel . |
| EnableInterrupt(ushort, ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType, uint) | Enables interrupts of the type you specify for the interruptTargetNode you specify, and assigns the interrupt signal the specified interruptConstantValue . |
| EnableInterrupt(ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType, BaseNode) | Enables interrupts of the type you specify and assigns the interrupt signal the value of the specified interruptChannel . This method sends the interrupts to all nodes on the reflective memory network. |
| EnableInterrupt(ReflectiveMemoryInterruptType, uint) | Enables interrupts of the type you specify and assigns the interrupt signal the specified interruptConstantValue . This method sends the interrupts to all nodes on the reflective memory network. |
| GetDataChannels() | Accesses the top-level Data Channels folder under the reflective memory device, which contains all data channels and subfolders. |
| GetInformationChannels() | Accesses the Information Channels section of the reflective memory device, which contains the device's Late Count channels. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI

### GetDataChannels()

Gets an array that contains the [ReflectiveMemoryDataChannel](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememorydatachannel.html) elements from the current [ReflectiveMemoryDataChannels](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememorydatachannels.html) section. This method gets the individual defined data channels for the reflective memory device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.VeriStand.SystemDefinitionAPI](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi.html)

public [ReflectiveMemoryDataChannel](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememorydatachannel.html)[] GetDataChannels()

#### Remarks

Note

Modifications you make to the contents of this list apply to the system definition. However, modifications you make to the array container, such as by calling Array.SetValue() or Array.Clear(), have no effect on the system definition.

#### Returns

An array that contains the [ReflectiveMemoryDataChannel](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememorydatachannel.html) elements from the current [ReflectiveMemoryDataChannels](nationalinstruments-veristand-systemdefinitionapi-reflectivememorydatachannels.html) section.

Parent topic:

ReflectiveMemoryDataChannels Class
